#  Test positions for CHA-Solver, taken from queries the community has

#  The initial two characters represent the expected classification
#  of the FEN with respect to winnability:
#
#     WB : if both players can helpmate
#     W- : if only White can helpmate
#     -B : if only Black can helpmate
#     -- : if no player can helpmate (dead draw)
#
